1)  
**Words on the 56th Birthday of the Teacher**  
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is February 5, 1976, the 6th day of the 1st month in the lunar calendar. This day marks the 56th birthday of this son, and the 33rd birthday of your beloved daughter.  
In 1960, our family, following the name of the True Parents, made a new start on this earth, and after 16 years of being established in your will, we are able to celebrate this birthday today, a historical day in 1976, in accordance with your providence. I first want to express my gratitude before you, Father.  
May you savor all these circumstances and this ceremony. I know that countless humanity living on this earth cannot celebrate the day of the birth of the True Parents. I also understand that many spirits in the spirit world cannot celebrate the day of the birth of the True Parents.  
This day is a day that connects heaven and earth, more significant than any historical day or the day when countless people were born. When we think about the fact that this day is a day to celebrate and commemorate the birth of parents, I know that heaven and earth recognize it as a day representing a new historical turning point where the spirit world and the physical world become one.  
Father, as I think about how much I have anticipated this ceremony, may you willingly celebrate this day. May you bless the countless good spirits in the spirit world who are centered on your name. May you bless the countless descendants born on this earth, inheriting their achievements, so that they may resolve the sorrow of not being able to commemorate the day of the birth of the True Parents on this earth.  
All descendants born on this earth do not know the day of the birth of the True Parents, but may you grant them the grace to celebrate this day together with God, centered on their ancestors, under the foundation of this earth.  
In your love, centered on the True Parents, as we think about the fact that this is a new historical time in front of your will to complete the ideal of creation you desired, may you rejoice, Father. May the entire spirit world also rejoice, and may your glory reach the earthly world so that all hearts of mankind can rejoice.  
Father, from 1960 until now, we have transcended the standard of individual perfection through the family foundation, passing through the first and second seven-year courses, transcending the national standard, connecting with the spiritual world of the Christian cultural realm, and now we are entering this historical time heading toward the third seven-year course. I earnestly hope that you bless the members in New York and the worldwide Unification Church as they prepare and organize for the time when heaven can finally take offensive action regarding this land, aiming for the Yankee Stadium event and the Washington event in 1976.  
At this time, I ask you to remember the members in Korea, as well as the countless young children in Japan, the United States, and the 123 nations. Although they cannot participate in this ceremony, may you grant them blessings many times over, so that they may fulfill their historical responsibilities. May they become children who are not ashamed, as they represent humanity and take responsibility for the Unification Church, becoming the vanguard of liberation for both humanity and the spirit world.  
Thus, as the founding warriors of the heavenly nation, may they lay the cornerstone correctly and complete the creative world you desire on the right foundation for future generations. I earnestly hope and wish that they can realize the heavenly kingdom on earth by practicing your love.  
Therefore, we must conclude the history of goodness left behind by the prophets and sages of the historical age who shed blood for their faith. We know that the day must come quickly when we can offer everything to you and sing the victory song along with the name of the True Parents, despite the chaos and turmoil of the world. We understand that we cannot stop our solemn responsibility to advance, risking our lives, regardless of the path of persecution we face.  
We know that not only America but the entire world is in turmoil right now. As we face this reality, may the Unification Church members, as the vanguard of heaven, become those who are not ashamed. Moreover, I earnestly ask that the 36 families, 72 families, 124 families, the 430 families, and the 777 families gathered here in Korea, as well as the 1800 families, unite under God's love and march toward your nation, becoming the eternal and indestructible ranks blessed by heaven.  
May you accept the joy of this day, Father. I thank you that today, as a son and daughter with the name of the True Parents, I can celebrate this historic birthday without being defeated or failing on the path of suffering.  
1976 is indeed a significant year that marks a cosmic transition, which is why we are holding this unification ceremony. Today, February 5, coincides with the beginning of spring in this country. I earnestly ask that this day, as the Unification Church enters a new spring, may it serve as an opportunity to resolve the sorrows of the ages and transition from the winter of resentment to the joyful spring of glorious times.  
Please bless your children gathered here. Representing all nations and all people, may this joy of celebrating the day of the birth of the True Parents be established as a condition for the indemnification of the sorrows of all spirits in the spirit world and those on earth who do not share this intention. May you exercise your sovereign authority so that they can be governed under the name of the True Parents. I earnestly hope and wish that you will transition to a time when the descendants of the evil parents can be blessed before the descendants of the good parents, allowing them to exercise the rights of the firstborn.  
Today, on the day of the birth of the True Parents, I declare that all spirits in the spirit world and descendants on earth will become one under your permission. Following the connections of the one family, the connections of the True Parents' family, and the connections of your love representing God, may enemies unite and the divided tribes and nations become one, advancing toward a world of unification. I earnestly hope and wish that you will directly govern this process in both spirit and flesh.  
May you fulfill your will, and may this day become a day that can be commemorated with joy, receiving your blessings in glory. I earnestly ask that you grant blessings a million times over to all those who pray and admire for this day.  
I thank you for allowing us to joyfully welcome this day in your name, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. (Recitation of the conclusion and cheers of "Mansei")  
<Words> Since we are scheduled to meet at 10 o'clock in Sutak-ri, I will briefly introduce the main content before you. As you know, today marks the 57th birthday of the Teacher and the 34th birthday of the Mother.  
At this time, we are at a historical turning point where heaven can decisively achieve victory. Looking back once again, it has already been 16 years since we held our marriage ceremony in 1960 under difficult circumstances, but today, as we hold this birthday celebration on the victorious foundation of heaven, I see historical significance in this event.  
Moreover, this year is… The United States is the blessed foundation of Western civilization, centered on the spiritual Christian world established due to Jesus' failure to achieve his purpose during his three-year ministry, leading to his crucifixion. This year marks the second year of the Unification Church's global three-year course, which aims to achieve what Jesus could not accomplish centered on the national standard.  
Since the first seven-year course began on April 1, 1960, we are currently in the first year of the third seven-year course. That is why, as you know, we have chosen May 1976, the first month of the second year of the third seven-year course, to hold the Yankee Stadium event. This second year corresponds to the second year of Jesus' public ministry. All events leading to Jesus' crucifixion were determined in this second year. It was necessary for the nation and Judaism to unite and transition toward heaven, moving toward the world of the heavenly kingdom on earth. However, due to the crucifixion, the cultural direction shifted from Western civilization back to Asia, and we have seen this flow until now.  
We must indemnify the sorrow of that time centered on America during this three-year period. As you know, the Christian world and the Unification Church are completely at odds with each other. What does this mean? It is a reality similar to the complete opposition of Judaism to Jesus in the past, which is now occurring globally.  
As you know, indemnity and restoration cannot be accomplished by God alone. In the midst of the opposition between God and Satan, there must be a responsible leader who can decide whether to side with Satan or heaven. Who must make that decisive responsibility? It must be a person. It must be Adam. In other words, it must be someone in the Abel position. From this perspective, the Yankee Stadium event and the Washington event are seen as crucial turning points in history that can bring decisive victory.  
**The Significance of the Celebration of the True Parents' Birthday**  
Even the spirits in the spirit world say that June 1976 is a time of global transition, which aligns with the providence. At such a time, many spirits in the spirit world and countless people on earth wish to be born as the descendants of the True Parents, receiving God's love through such parents.  
So what is their sorrow? It is that their birthday is not a day that God can celebrate. Therefore, their life is one that cannot be praised by God. The spirits in the spirit world are, of course, in such a position, but the 4 billion people on earth and the members of the Unification Church are also in that position.  
At this time, when we must transition to one world, what is the important issue we must realize? Centered on the day of the birth of the True Parents, we must go through three years to celebrate the birthday of the True Parents. We believe that without going through this three-year period, they cannot have their own birthday.  
What this means is that because Adam fell, he must go through the three stages of rebirth, growth, and perfection to be resurrected again. Therefore, during this three-year period, we must establish connections with the birthday of the True Parents to have our own birthday. That is why this ceremony today provides the benefit of participating in the celebration of the day of the birth of the True Parents. Do you understand what I mean?  
Because of this, the spirits in the spirit world and countless people on earth who do not share this intention will have the condition to commemorate the day of the birth of the True Parents. Thus, after the conclusion of the third seven-year course in 1981, all spirits in the spirit world and humans will enter a time of blessings where they can have their own birthday. This is how we see it. In this sense, today's birthday celebration has profound historical significance that you must understand.  
By serving in this place to celebrate the day of the birth of the True Parents, the spirit world and the physical world will be connected as brothers. By celebrating together, the spirit world and the earth will establish a brotherly relationship.  
Now is the time for the spirit world, in the position of Cain, to serve the earth, in the position of Abel. Until now, the spirit world, in the position of Cain, has dominated humanity. The spiritual beings have controlled all humans, using them for their own benefit. However, when we stand in the position of children centered on the True Parents, that time will pass.  
According to God's law, we are entering a time where the order of precedence is established, centered on those who are closer to heaven, establishing the principles of order. The humans living on earth have been in the position of the second Abel, but like Jacob, they have taken the birthright and received blessings, leading to a time of transition where now the earth's people can dominate the spirit world, rather than the spirit world dominating the earth.  
If this is misused, it will lead to interference from the spirit world. This is how it will be. From this perspective, the many spiritual beings on earth who have experienced everything spiritually will no longer use those experiences for their livelihood, whether judging people's destinies or foreseeing the future for profit. That time will pass, and if they continue in that way, they will bring misfortune upon themselves.  
Ultimately, it will be a time for the people on earth. It will be a time for the sons and daughters of God. When we look at the spirit world itself, it corresponds to the angelic world before the creation of Adam and Eve. This archangel has ultimately ruled over humanity. This is the fallen world. We must overturn this.  
The angel was created before Adam. He came first and ruled over Adam's domain. Until now, Adam has been in a position of no value because...
In other words, there is no standard for the existence of Adam, only the angelic realm. Because of this position, all people on earth today have been dwelling in the world of the angelic realm. They have been under the dominion of the spirit world. Do you understand what I mean?

However, now it is different. The True Parents have come and established the standard of victory... To say that the standard of victory has been established means that standing in the historical Abel position, all of humanity has been placed in the Cain position, and this has been restored through indemnity, returning to the position of the firstborn.

What is the path that the returning Lord must take? It is to ascend from the era of rebirth to the era of growth, in other words, from the era of Adam to the era of Jesus, and then back to the era of completion. This is the path of restoring what Adam failed to achieve. It means turning things upside down. So, from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world, what are we trying to find? First, because Adam failed, I must stand in the position of the second Adam, and although I am in the position of the second son, I must first step on the standard of the firstborn and rise to the position of the firstborn in the name of God.

Today is the day when the fallen descendants who were separated from the True Parents are connected.

So what has the Unification Church been doing until now? It has been engaging in the work of restoring the firstborn rights from the Abel position, in the direction of individual, family, tribal, national, and global standards. Therefore, when we are restored to the position of the firstborn in the name of God, we enter into the realm where God can exercise His dominion. This is how we see it.

From this perspective, what is happening at this point today? It is a transition. With the transition, the spirit world and the physical world... Until now, what has been the grievance of the spirit world? It has been that they could not commemorate the day of the birth of the True Parents. Although the True Parents were born on earth, there was no connection. This must be commemorated. With the condition of commemorating this connection, they will finally establish the justification of sons and daughters, and thus restore their own day of birth. This is how it will happen. In this sense, you must understand that today’s gathering is a place where both the spirit world and the physical world pay attention and commemorate together.

Because of this, there can be no failure in the Unification Church. The more we are attacked, the fiercer the attacks are, the more victories we will receive from now on. This is how I see it. Therefore, we are preparing for the Yankee Stadium event in the United States this year, and there must be a global event. This is our expectation. There must be a global event.

At this time of transition... Until now, even though Satan has attacked our church, it has only been verbal attacks. There has been no physical violence to break our church. However, the bombing incident that occurred in France has turned out to be a good condition for indemnity, for heaven to step over it.

The fact that the Unification Church was bombed in France means that the Unification Church is establishing a historical condition for indemnity... It means that Satan has attacked a realm that should not be attacked. This has become a condition for us to take the offensive.

Therefore, all these events that have occurred are not coincidental. Ultimately, heaven is establishing external conditions for the Unification Church to win. All opposition and persecution... If we can just get past April and into June, I believe it will completely turn into favorable results for our Unification Church. And if we get past August of this year, the Unification Church will create a new environment in America. On the day of the Yankee Stadium event, I believe that the victory of this three-year course will be completed at this year’s Washington event. Thus, in the next three years, we will enter a period where we can completely strengthen our internal organization within the United States. This is the perspective of the teacher.

Because such results have been determined, it has started from Korea, as you know, with the Unification Ceremony held on the first day of the lunar month. The Unification Ceremony is about setting the direction. Until now, the teacher has been dealing with individuals, families, tribes, and nations in this way, but in America, we have not been able to establish a position centered on the direction of the world. In establishing the central nation of the world, the direction must be set from a national position, so the teacher went to America in 1972 and presented the direction, thereby establishing the global direction.

Thus, while connecting individuals, families, tribes, nations, the world, and heaven, this connection has been centered on our Unification Church. However, the connection with established churches, nations, the world, and the spirit world has not been established. This was the purpose of the Unification Ceremony on the first day of the lunar month.

Now, this connection has been made. The unified path has been opened. What does this mean? It means that for those who are not fallen within the realm of the unfallen world, a path to heaven has been created. A highway has been established. As long as one does not fall, they can walk this path.

Because of this, a unified path has emerged, just like in the Garden of Eden... There must be parents, and there must be children. There must be parents, and where do the children connect? The spirits in the spirit world are also in the position of children, and all people on earth are also in the position of children, but where do they connect? They connect at this point. Do you understand what I mean?

This is a historical position where parents and children can be connected. Therefore, if possible, today’s birthday should be celebrated with more significance than celebrating the birthday of any king. This is the teacher's heart. We must prepare with more sincerity than that shown in celebrating the birthday of any king or sovereign in the historical era. Also, those who commemorate this day should attend with more sincerity than any historical loyal subjects or virtuous women, and with the heart of filial piety. It is such a day.

This day is the day when all fallen descendants who were separated from the True Parents are finally connected. It is finally here that they will be connected. Therefore, when the three-year course ends, all people of the world will be drawn to the name of the True Parents without even realizing it. That time will come. This is because the original mind knows this. Because the Unification Church has not yet laid the foundation of this purpose, even when hearing the name of the True Parents, their hearts have not moved. However, if we just pass about three years from now and lay the foundation of victory in America, by the time we surpass 1980 and lay a complete foundation, many people will flock to the Unification Church without needing to evangelize.

Also, the spirit world will not remain idle. The spirit world is in the position of the archangel. What must the archangel do? They must cooperate with God’s and Adam’s will. That is the archangel. Then what is God’s will? It is to complete Adam. Adam’s will is to complete himself. What does that completion mean? What does it mean to complete the ideal of creation? It means making the realm of Satan completely nonexistent. Because Eden was a place where the conditions for accusation remained, it was not seen as heaven.

We must surpass the standard that can suppress the communist realm until the third seven-year course.

Then how will we remove such a realm of accusation during the teacher's lifetime? This is the fateful task. Therefore, the teacher believes that by the 1980s, we will surpass a certain standard, and if we act quickly, we can completely defeat the communist realm, and the world will be directed within this realm of unification, and all humanity will come to understand that this is the only way.

If we achieve victory during this three-year period, it will happen without any problems. However, if we do not achieve victory during this three-year period and if we bring about failure here, it will be a big problem. From the 1980s to the 2000s, we must have another 20-year period. This will be purely a time of struggle against the communists. We must go through this 20-year process of fighting against the communists. This is what pertains to the year 2000, and during that period, there will be much bloodshed. Many people will be sacrificed, including Christians and, of course, the Unification Church. It will truly be a matter of whether we survive or not, a secondary path. It will not be a spiritual hell but a physical hell and heaven...

Therefore, regardless of what sacrifices may be required, we must surpass the standard that can suppress the communist realm until the third seven-year course. If we do not surpass this standard, we cannot establish the realm of victory from heaven. It means we cannot win. In other words, if we are invaded by the communist realm, even if it is a conditional invasion, it becomes an invasion by Satan, so we must lay the foundation to completely suppress the communist realm and go beyond it.

From this perspective, the fact that the teacher is currently engaged in the work of organizing the third seven-year course in America is entirely for the purpose of achieving victory. With the consolidation of the internal foundation centered on the House of Representatives and the Senate, how do we strengthen the anti-communist system nationwide? This is the mission we must undertake from now on in the third seven-year course.

By doing this, on the day we achieve victory in America, all humanity will unconsciously see Reverend Moon as a beacon of hope, as a light of hope... The direction we are heading will be seen as a place of hope by all humanity. Therefore, to do decisive work during this three-year period, we are holding the Unification Ceremony and commemorating the day of the True Parents’ birth to establish the connection of the children here in Korea. From the perspective of providential history, you must understand that this is a great historical turning point. You have attended such a gathering.

After this ceremony, what will you do? What should you do? With the mindset of running ahead of any loyal subjects or martyrs, we must advance through the third seven-year course. In other words, during the third seven-year course, the Unification Church members must not be accused by anyone saying, “What is that? What is that?”

The third seven-year course is a realm where God can indirectly exercise His dominion. It corresponds to the realm of completion within rebirth, growth, and completion, so in this realm, God exercises indirect dominion.

Then who moves God? Who must move this world? Adam must move. Do you understand what I mean? Adam must move. God must be moved by Adam, and the world must be moved by Adam. Before Adam, both God and the world are dependent on him. This is the position.

God’s purpose of creation is fulfilled through Adam, and the ideal of creation of all things is realized through Adam, so God is dependent on Adam, and all things, including animals, are dependent on Adam. What this means is that when the Unification Church enters the third seven-year course, the whole must rely on the Unification Church. In other words, this nation and this world are dependent on us, and God is also dependent on us. Do you understand what I mean?

Until now, the first and second seven-year courses have been the responsibility of the teacher. The fact that you are in a position to celebrate the birthday of the True Parents means that you have become the children of the True Parents, which means you have surpassed the realm of rebirth and growth. It means you are in a position that has surpassed that. What kind of position is that? It is a position that must be better than anyone in the satanic world. The era of being accused before them has passed. Therefore, it is time to take responsibility in a public position and sacrifice toward a direction that heaven and earth can look upon and support. Do you understand?

From this perspective, how should you live? You must live a life that is completely unrelated to the world. We must truly lead the way and ensure that they cannot interfere at all. The atmosphere must change. No one should be able to follow us. We must rise early and return late... With this mindset, we must surpass the third seven-year course. We must be more active than the world’s communist parties, and regardless of how strong the environment is, we must be stronger than that strong environment. This is the responsibility of all of you as we go through the three-year course.

After this is over, there will be no need for evangelism. The spirit world will do all of that. Through whose name? Through the name of the Parents. All humanity is the sons and daughters of the Parents, so who will do it? It is a history of re-creation, so standing in the position of God, who created, the Parents will send the archangels to re-create the sons and daughters. They will all be engaged in that work. You must understand that the completion stage, where such decisive standards must be fully established, is the third seven-year course. Do you understand?

Therefore, during this period, especially women, who have given birth and raised children until now, must stand in a sacrificial position even when giving birth. Being sacrificial does not mean you should not eat. It means you must stand in a public position. Many women have given birth until now, but you must be different from those women. You must be different. That is why I have told mothers to endure and move forward even if it is difficult. The time has come for that. In every aspect, the Unification Church must establish a standard that is better than anything in the satanic world during this third seven-year course.

Live in a manner like the Levites.

In terms of national standards, until now, nations have been divided and have become enemy states, deviating from the direction of history, and we must break through this internal standard. That is why since last year, we have been sending missionaries paired with people from enemy nations. America, Japan, Germany, all of them were enemies 30 years ago. Can they unite more than with their own mothers and fathers? Can they unite more than as brothers of the world? They can unite. They can unite because the spirit world teaches them. Therefore, they can go abroad and unite beyond the satanic world and stand in a position to pledge loyalty before heaven’s will. You must think about how the missionaries are working from that position.

I believe that our Korean leaders must also be involved in this. Therefore, if possible, during this period, I plan to have 36 families, 72 families, and 124 families visit the missionaries working abroad to strengthen the training organization. We must establish this condition. Such conditions have not been established domestically. We cannot continue living as we have been habitually doing. This time, I heard that they decided to pay 150,000 won as a salary, but that must be reported to the teacher! It is not something the association president can decide on their own! It must not be easier than before. In my opinion, until the third seven-year course, we must make the Korean people suffer. We are trying to make them suffer. Why are we trying to make them suffer? We are making them suffer for the sake of the will. The priest does not receive a salary. Does the Bible say that the Levites received a salary? When God gives, they eat, and when He does not, they do not eat, even if they starve to death. That is the path the Levites have taken. The teacher knows this. The mindset of wanting to share equally with the world... This is not the Levite way. If possible, the world...
You have to live on one-third, just enough to not die. It means to survive on that. This is the teacher's assertion. 

It's not because I hate you. It's to bring the blessings of the world to you. If you live well and receive a salary just like the world, the path to receiving blessings is blocked. That's all about principles. Even if we die or fail, we must live by principles. Is receiving a salary a privilege of the Levites? We must eat and live through the church in any way possible. 

It's fortunate that the teacher has laid the economic foundation; otherwise, if you had played around through other institutions, you would have been completely caught. You would be completely playing in the world of Satan. You need to understand that. Therefore, as long as the teacher is running ahead, you must also follow that path. Isn't that right? If you've gone far, you must follow the path you've taken anyway. It's the same. 

If the teacher had set your salaries in Korea so that you could live without spending a single cent of American money, and if we said we would provide the money the teacher needs, then you wouldn't be bound by conditions. However, the teacher, regardless of that, focuses on personal matters... This indicates a difference in ideology and intention with the teacher. You need to understand that. It's not about a few bucks of salary being an issue. It's about the principle. 

Until we go through the third seven-year course, we Koreans must suffer. We must suffer. Especially, the 36 families must suffer, and the 124 families must suffer. Now that I have established a company, everyone is abandoning the church and going to the company. In the end, who will be left? Everyone will run away. Eventually, even the association president and top executives will say, "Send us as company presidents." I foresee that. When that day comes... I believe that such people cannot receive heavenly blessings. That deviates from the principles. 

If the third seven-year course is a sacrificial course, the whole world is watching, and you are the problem. Just the other day, you raised salaries without even consulting me... Where is that kind of law? It's not that the teacher is stingy with money. It's because I think of your descendants receiving blessings for thousands and tens of thousands of years, eternally. Nowadays, asking for a car or something... Such words are, in my view, truly frightening. What about a car? 

Even though you already know the intention, even though you know what the third seven-year course is... We must understand that we need to become sacrifices. At this point where we must become sacrifices, we must stand in a sacrificial position, shedding blood and sweat, and achieve victory in the global field during the third seven-year course. If we do that, even if they don't want to, foreigners will do everything for us. That's why I have prepared the economic rights. If that hadn't been done, you would have been completely caught. You would be said to be without intention. 

In light of that, who must be the first to overcome in this global transition period? You must be the first to overcome. That's how I see it. I intend to educate and feed your children. However, I believe that the parents must suffer. Then why shouldn't the children suffer? They are the second generation. The parents are the first generation. The first generation must sacrifice for the second generation because they are at the archangel level. Sacrificing the archangel to save the son is God's will, and that is the principle of creation. 

You must not deviate from the principled position for your own future to be smooth. Since it has come to this, you must have that mindset. The money that goes through the teacher is fearsome money. It's fearsome money. Look. To earn that money, if you look at the Japanese members... Among them, there are those who have worn a single pair of underwear for seven years, a woman who wears clothes that cannot be shown to anyone and is playing around. You must understand that this is a terrifying thing. You would completely lose blessings to Japan. There may not be much in Japan now, but when the spirits of the Korean people go to the spiritual world, losing the authority to boast about their lineage and standing in a position where the spirits of the Japanese people can boast is a shameful fact. It's a shameful fact. 

Now, you too must connect with the association president this year, just like during the Day of Hope festival, and engage in that activity. The association president must go to the regions several times a month to hold lectures and guide. If he cannot, he must appoint someone to strengthen the mobilization team, whether it be in the military or in each church, to maintain that atmosphere and unify it. You must stand in a position to overcome the third seven-year course centered on the nation before anyone else. You must understand that this is your mission during the third seven-year course. 

The 36 families, 72 families, and 124 families must go out to the global front lines. So what should the parents do? They must open the way for their children. What does that mean? Last April, I gathered the mobilization team and held the Day of Hope festival. That opened the way for you. Until now, you have faced sorrow and difficulties, but if you maintain that atmosphere centered on the standard after this event, the public opinion about the teacher will become nationwide... Through our Day of Hope festival, we have established a good foundation that can carry forward the atmosphere that the whole nation has come to know. You must engage in activities that can carry that forward.

Why were humans born?

February 8, 1976, Sunday, at the main church.

6) The Goal of Restoration

The sorrows of history, the sorrows of the past must be settled in the present, and if there are sorrows in the present, they must be settled in the future. When we think about how much time we spend worrying about the whole and the will compared to the time we spend worrying about ourselves, we must recognize that it is a shameful fact that everything centered on ourselves occupies our time.

We have come to know that there is no way to contribute to the world before transcending the Republic of Korea. <Words> This morning, I would like to speak briefly on the topic of "The Goal of Restoration."

The life of Adam and Eve, which was to be the standard of human culture
Today, we know that humanity is in distress. We are at a stage where we must think about what the global path humanity must take in the future will be, even if we dislike it.

From this perspective, the Republic of Korea is no exception. Since the Republic of Korea stands in such a position, it is natural that you, as members of the Republic of Korea, cannot be exceptions either.

The confusion that has arisen is ultimately due to the fall. Because of the fall...
This is the result that has come to be. What is sown must be reaped. We know that we reap what we sow. Humanity's ancestors were wrongly sown due to their fall. Although the original purpose of humanity was to sow true ideals, because they were wrongly sown, we cannot help but think that we must go for a wrong purpose.

What does that mean? It means that such results came about because of the fall. Then we must consider what would have happened if there had been no fall.

If Adam and Eve had not fallen, they would undoubtedly have become the sons and daughters of God, true sons and daughters of God. If they had become true sons and daughters of God, they would have passed through childhood, youth, adulthood, and old age without falling, becoming unfallen grandparents. Then there would have been unfallen grandparents, unfallen parents, unfallen couples, and of course, unfallen children, including infants, who would have grown old and died without falling. A standard model of human beings who should not fall would have emerged in the human world. Moreover, because they lived without falling, a new lifestyle centered on God would have emerged through Adam and Eve. This is an undeniable fact.

Then, as unfallen children centered on God, they would have undoubtedly lived with God as their parent, receiving God's love. In other words, from childhood to old age, they would have lived their lives on this earth under God's protective love, and it is certain that they would have lived their entire lives in that environment. Therefore, when they were born, they would have been born under God's love, and while living, they would have lived under God's love, and even in death, they would die under God's love.

In that case, the life of Adam would have been, perhaps, limited in scope at that time, but it would not have been a limited standard, whether personal, familial, or tribal. It would have been a standard that transcended all environments, establishing a tradition. The life of Adam would have been a standard lifestyle, a model lifestyle for all future generations of humanity.

For this reason, individual perfection becomes a model for the perfection of families to come. Furthermore, the model of family perfection, when many descendants and tribes are born, will be set as the standard for tribal perfection. The standard for tribal perfection will become the standard for national perfection, and the standard for national perfection will become the standard for world perfection.

If such a world had started and such historical significance had developed, then today, humanity would not have become a confused world that has lost direction and is facing despair.

This is not originally what God intended. The reality we see today is not the original design with which God created humanity. It is something beyond this. It is only natural to conclude that if there is an absolute being beyond this, the standard that the absolute being envisioned must have been a world of a higher dimension.

Therefore, we can conclude that the life of Adam, as such a standard, represents the entirety of human history. What Adam lived out would have been the tradition of today's human culture, and that tradition would have become a cultural standard that could not change with the changes of historical eras.

Why is that? Because it is a life course determined by God's love, and nothing can change that life course beyond God's love. Isn't that so? The love you have cannot be changed by any external stimulus. We hope for that.

Today, for those who engage in worldly love, it may seem that external issues like power, money, or knowledge can change things, but the place where the relationship of love established under the absolute love of God exists is a high-dimensional place that cannot be changed by anything external.

When we look at it this way, the culture that Adam lived in, no matter how long history may be, could become the origin that can move that history. Why? Because God's love accompanied Adam's life. Thus, we can confidently conclude this. True love is eternal, true love is unchanging, true love is absolute. Therefore, today humanity seeks true love.

If humanity had not fallen and had become one with God, then because they would have been in the realm of true love, that love would have been eternal, that love would have been unchanging, and that love would have been absolute and unique, forming a cultural background. If he had praised, he would have praised as a model representing humanity. What he lived would have become the standard that humanity desires.

Why is that? Because it is a stage of life that has established a relational connection with God's love. Adam and Eve were made into a couple centered on that love. That couple cannot be the standard path for humanity to follow. The methods of education they used to raise their children would have been an educational system that humanity today could inherit 100% as it is. And all the kinship relationships, even in a small tribal environment, would have been historically significant. This is beyond question. If God came from the East, He could freely pass through the Adam family to the West, and from the North to the South, in any direction, there would be no obstacles in passing through the Adam family or the Adam tribe. No matter which of the 360 degrees or angles one chooses to go, they would go straight without colliding with that family or tribe, welcoming them, and it would have been an environment where everything could respond and interact harmoniously.

From that perspective, the Unification Church today concludes that when Adam and Eve were created, there was a divine ideal of creation. What is that divine ideal? It is a family where the whole can harmonize within God's love. That is the kind of family that must be formed. So, when asked what God's will is, people in general religions might say, "God's will is God's will." But they cannot clarify it. When asked what God's will is, saying "God's will is God's will" is not enough.

Once, I called a famous theologian in Korea and asked him, "What is God's will?" He gave a rather profound answer: "God's will is easy if it is easy, and difficult if it is difficult." But that is not sufficient. What is God's will? We in the Unification Church must conclude that God's will is to fulfill the purpose of creation! It must be so. Since humanity was created within God's will, what is God's will? It is to fulfill humanity. In other words, it is to fulfill the purpose of creation. What will be done by fulfilling the purpose of creation? It is to realize the ideal of creation.

When we talk about the purpose of creation, we are referring to individuals. You see, when we talk about the purpose of creation, there is a purpose for men and a purpose for women, but just having the individual purpose of creation is not enough. It must be idealized. An ideal is not something that can be achieved alone. An ideal is not something that can be achieved alone. Isn't that right? The ideal world of humanity must come when people of all races, regardless of skin color, live together as one.

You must understand that without this heart, you cannot cross this boundary. (Pointing to what was written) Personal heart, family heart, tribal heart, national heart, state heart; these must be for God, for humanity, for the world, and you must transcend them, as this is your undeniable destiny of restoration.

You must understand that such a law, more fearsome than the law of causality, applies to your life and eternal journey, and I hope you do not get caught in it, but rather be liberated from it and become the sons and daughters of God as I conclude my words.

<Prayer> No one knew that your high and precious will would go through such a painful twist. Now, we, who are insignificant, have come to understand your original heart and your wishes. We have come to understand what your ideal of creation is.

Father! What is the limit of restoration, what is the standard of the goal of restoration? It is the heart. I have come to understand how necessary it is to have words that can communicate the heart, thoughts that can communicate the heart, a lifestyle that can communicate the heart, and a life course that can communicate the heart. I have come to realize that those who can do so will never fail. I have come to understand that if this fails, your will cannot be fulfilled on this earth.

Through today’s words, I have come to know what the goal of restoration is. The heart, and how we should move forward centered on that heart, I sincerely hope that we can become children who can critically reflect on ourselves in a position of self-examination and, while criticizing ourselves from God's perspective, can have the joy of expanding our own value.

Father! I earnestly ask you to bless the many tribes and nations that gather in your name today, and especially the children in Japan and the United States, and the many Unification Church members scattered around the world, with the same blessing, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

Now, let’s sing the song "Man, Man" once. When we say "Man," it might not be fun for the women. No matter how good a woman is, if the man does not restore himself, the woman cannot restore herself, forever. It is when we say "Man, Man" that the woman comes to restoration. Do you understand? "Yes." So, in that sense, I can attach my character to "my man." It can be "my man," right? Don’t say "my wife," just add a character and say "my man," and that works. Then it connects. So, it’s not that they all have to get married and go. Right? Start!

1. The man running in the wilderness, man, man
Today in North Gando, tomorrow in Mongolia
Flowing and flowing like the floating water lily
How many years has it been since I left my hometown?
Facing the sunset (facing the sunset), run (run), man (man)
A man's life is not regrettable.
2. The man of the endless wilderness, man, man
Embracing the fierce winds of the Black Dragon River
This is the battlefield of the South
With a smiling face and fluttering beard
Cutting through the cold wind (cold wind), run (run), man (man)
A man's life has no regrets (repeated twice) *
